style=\"line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">利用带刻度的试纸条吸取眼泪用于研究，图中的被试是一只大嘴𫛭。这种纸条也会用在人类的眼科检查中 | Arianne P. Oriá</span></p></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">眼泪对维持眼睛健康起着重要作用，但在此之前，只有很少几种哺乳动物的眼泪成分得到过研究。这一次，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">巴西研究者从7个鸟类与爬行动物物种身上收集了眼泪样本，分析了它们的成分，以及眼泪蒸发后产生的结晶形态</strong>[3]。总的来说，这些物种与人的泪液组成其实相当相似。不过，不同动物眼泪中蛋白质、尿素与电解质离子的含量依然存在很多细节差异，蒸发时产生的结晶形态也很不同。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6666667\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/icZklJrRfHgD16ldy07wibx7IrvPqmXkgGSnrY1AMicebRZPsxxJTb2umsNSmoC6KRQVGXibhRgqSneIHBmeicn4f6w/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">另一位接受眼泪采集的动物被试——一只仓鸮 | Arianne P. Oriá</span></p></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">分析不同动物的眼泪不仅能了解泪液的演化，也可以从中找出能让泪膜更稳定的泪液配方，这或许能帮助人们更好地治疗干眼症之类的眼科疾病。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding-right: 6px;padding-bottom: 6px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-top: 6px;display: inline-block;background-color: rgb(237, 242, 238);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: -6px;margin-bottom: -6px;margin-left: 6px;background-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 6px;padding-left: 6px;font-size: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> 捕食瞬间 </p></section></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">这块9900万年前的琥珀，凝固了幽冥蚁捕食的瞬间。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.562963\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/icZklJrRfHgD16ldy07wibx7IrvPqmXkgGMvSAdGf13gD8NaW7T4sKjtp9GU4FxYqBMmpyw1NSiaib2lnAkRM5ibaJg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">NJIT; Chinese Academy of Sciences; University of Rennes, France</span></p></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">幽冥蚁是目前已知的最古老的蚂蚁，生活在白垩纪时期。现代蚂蚁口部的下颌骨是左右移动的，而幽冥蚁的下颌骨则是垂直移动，类似于人类下颚的张合。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在琥珀中，这种已经灭绝的长角幽冥蚁（<em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">Ceratomyrmex ellenbergeri</em>）用头上的角与尖锐的下颚抓住它的猎物——一种已经灭绝的与蟑螂有亲缘关系的昆虫（<em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">Caputoraptor elegans</em>）幼虫</strong>。这块琥珀展现了幽冥蚁的捕食方式，该研究发表于《当代生物学》[4]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding-right: 6px;padding-bottom: 6px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-top: 6px;display: inline-block;background-color: rgb(237, 242, 238);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: -6px;margin-bottom: -6px;margin-left: 6px;background-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 6px;padding-left: 6px;font-size: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> 明亮荧光 </p></section></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">通过一种简单的处理，研究者们制造出了目前最为明亮的荧光材料</span></strong><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">[5]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">这种十分明亮的固态荧光材料被称为“SMILES”，它是常见荧光染料与名叫“氰星”（Cyanostar）的环形分子共结晶的产物。它可以加入聚合物材料当中，通过3D打印等方式生产不同形态的产品。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6462963\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/icZklJrRfHgD16ldy07wibx7IrvPqmXkgGHtOQCVM34v3FSBLaNiaCtfkoTTHuIO2tqrgelbvkdia9jxL6ERuqTdfg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">使用SMILES的3D打印模型，在紫外光激发下发出荧光 | Amar Flood</span></p></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">过去，人们已经制造出了很多在溶液中发光良好的荧光染料。然而问题是，这些染料一旦进入固体形态，荧光效果就会大打折扣。这是因为固体状态下染料分子彼此“离得太近”，发生了被称为“电子耦合”的相互作用。而氰星的加入能帮助染料分子彼此隔离，从而维持高亮度的荧光效果。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;align-items: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"flex: 1 1 auto;height: 1px;background-color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section><section style=\"flex: 0 1 auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section opera-tn-ra-cell=\"_$.pages:0.layers:0.comps:29.col1\" style=\"padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.61;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">参考文献<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section><section style=\"flex: 1 1 auto;height: 1px;transform: matrix(-1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);background-color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;height: 180px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: left;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;color: rgb(205, 204, 204);line-height: 1.61;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p border-box;\">[5] https://www.cell.com/chem/fulltext/S2451-9294(20)30310-7</span></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p
